# Calisthenics Exercise Cards 1-50

Complete Card v2 authoring output for Cursor/import work.

Source basis: exercise_card_details_for_llm.md defines the Vortex Card v2 authoring workflow, canonical session phases, taxonomy tags, publish gates, Authoring JSON format, dosage/scaling/safety fields, and anti-patterns. The File Library also surfaced calisthenics-cards-1-50.mjs as an existing calisthenics card precedent. Purpose.txt was requested but was not located in the available File Library search results for this session; therefore, the work below is grounded in the Exercise Card Authoring Guide, the existing calisthenics card precedent, and exercise-selection expertise.


## Prepare & Access / Hand-Support Mobility

1. **Rocking Plank to Down Dog** - Bodyweight flow that opens calves, hamstrings, shoulders, and trunk while introducing light hand support.
2. **Quadruped Wrist Pronation Supination Shifts** - Low-load wrist and forearm access drill for hand-support preparation.
3. **Scapular Push-Up** - Straight-arm plank drill that activates serratus and teaches shoulder blade motion without elbow bending.
4. **Beast Hold** - Low hover hold that activates trunk, shoulders, hips, and foot pressure before crawls or strength work.
5. **Bear Crawl Prep** - Slow contralateral crawl pattern that prepares shoulders, wrists, trunk, hips, and feet for floor-based locomotion.
6. **Crab Reach** - Reverse tabletop reach that opens the front line while preparing posterior shoulder support and hip extension.
7. **World's Greatest Stretch to Plank** - Integrated lunge and plank flow that opens hips, hamstrings, T-spine, and shoulders before calisthenics work.
8. **Deep Squat Pry with Reach** - Controlled deep-squat mobility drill that builds ankle, hip, and thoracic access for bodyweight squat patterns.
9. **Hollow Body Hold** - Foundational bodyline hold that teaches rib-pelvis stacking, trunk tension, and lever control for calisthenics.
10. **Dead Bug** - Low-threat anti-extension drill that activates trunk control before floor, crawl, push-up, or hanging work.

## Movement Intelligence / Shape, Locomotion & Inversion

11. **Hollow Rock** - Dynamic hollow-body drill that teaches trunk tension, rocking control, and gymnastics shape awareness.
12. **Tuck-Up** - Tuck compression drill that builds coordinated trunk flexion, hip flexion, and controlled shape changes.
13. **V-Up Progression** - Advanced compression-bodyweight drill that builds coordinated trunk flexion, hip flexion, and pike/tuck control.
14. **Straddle Compression Lift** - Seated straddle compression drill that builds active hip flexion, adductor control, and trunk posture.
15. **Tuck L-Sit Hold** - Supported tuck hold that teaches shoulder depression, trunk compression, and bodyweight support control.
16. **Wall Walk** - Wall-assisted inversion entry that teaches hand walking, shoulder stacking, and bodyline control.
17. **Wall-Facing Handstand Hold** - Chest-to-wall handstand hold that develops overhead support, bodyline awareness, and safe inversion control.
18. **Wall-Facing Handstand Toe Pull** - Wall-facing handstand drill that teaches line awareness and controlled toe pressure away from the wall.
19. **Forward Roll to Stand** - Basic rolling transition that links trunk flexion, spatial orientation, and controlled return to standing.
20. **Lateral Ape Walk** - Lateral hand-foot locomotion drill that develops hip mobility, shoulder support, coordination, and rhythm.

## Capacity / Lower-Body Bodyweight Strength

21. **Prisoner Squat** - Hands-behind-head bodyweight squat that builds squat capacity, thoracic posture, and trunk control.
22. **Tempo Bodyweight Squat** - Bodyweight squat variation using slow tempo and pauses to build leg strength and control without external load.
23. **Split Squat** - Stationary unilateral squat pattern that develops single-leg strength, hip control, and repeatable knee tracking.
24. **Reverse Lunge** - Backward-stepping lunge that builds unilateral leg strength and deceleration control with lower forward knee stress than many forward lunges.
25. **Bulgarian Split Squat** - Rear-foot-elevated unilateral squat that increases bodyweight loading demand for the front leg.
26. **Step-Up** - Box-supported unilateral strength exercise that trains one-leg force production and controlled lowering.
27. **Cossack Squat** - Side-to-side squat variation that builds adductor strength, hip mobility, and frontal-plane control.
28. **Pistol Squat to Box** - Supported-depth single-leg squat progression that builds unilateral strength and control with a box target.
29. **Single-Leg Glute Bridge** - Floor-based unilateral hip-extension drill that builds glute strength and pelvis control.
30. **Glute Bridge Walkout** - Bridge walkout that gradually increases hamstring leverage while maintaining pelvis and trunk control.

## Capacity / Upper-Body Push, Pull & Core Strength

31. **Incline Push-Up** - Hands-elevated push-up regression that builds pressing strength while reducing load and preserving bodyline quality.
32. **Push-Up** - Foundational bodyweight press that builds chest, triceps, shoulder, and trunk strength in one integrated pattern.
33. **Close-Grip Push-Up** - Bodyweight pressing variation that emphasizes triceps, shoulder control, and tight plank position.
34. **Decline Push-Up** - Feet-elevated push-up that increases upper-body loading and anterior trunk demand.
35. **Pike Push-Up** - Bodyweight vertical-press progression that builds shoulders, triceps, and trunk control toward handstand pushing.
36. **Parallel-Bar Dip Progression** - Bodyweight dip progression that builds pressing strength through shoulder extension, elbow extension, and support control.
37. **Inverted Row** - Bodyweight horizontal pull that builds upper-back strength, grip, and trunk stiffness with scalable leverage.
38. **Strict Pull-Up** - Foundational vertical pulling exercise that builds lats, upper back, arms, grip, and trunk tension.
39. **Eccentric Pull-Up** - Slow-lowering pull-up progression that builds vertical pulling strength, grip, and tissue tolerance.
40. **Tuck Hanging Knee Raise** - Hanging knee raise that builds grip, shoulder control, anterior core strength, and hip flexion capacity.

## Resilience & Sustained Capacity / Anti-Movement, Crawls & Conditioning

41. **Plank Shoulder Tap** - Alternating shoulder-tap plank that trains anti-rotation, shoulder support, and weight-shift control.
42. **Side Plank** - Lateral trunk hold that builds shoulder support, oblique strength, and pelvis control.
43. **Reverse Plank** - Supine-facing support hold that builds posterior shoulder tolerance, hip extension, and trunk control.
44. **Active Hang** - Hanging shoulder-control drill that builds grip, scapular depression, and overhead tissue tolerance.
45. **Flexed-Arm Hang** - Top-position isometric hang that builds vertical pulling strength, grip, and scapular control.
46. **Mountain Climber** - Plank-based conditioning drill that trains trunk stiffness, hip drive, shoulder support, and repeatable coordination.
47. **Squat Thrust** - Simple bodyweight conditioning movement that trains plank-to-squat transitions without the push-up or jump of a full burpee.
48. **Burpee Step-Back** - Low-impact calisthenics conditioning movement that trains full-body transition capacity without a jump or push-up requirement.
49. **Skater Step** - Low-impact lateral step pattern that develops lateral rhythm, balance, and sustained side-to-side movement without high plyometric demand.
50. **Crab Walk** - Reverse quadruped locomotion that develops shoulder support, hip extension, coordination, and full-body work capacity.
